            function containsStr($str, $substr) {
                return strpos($str, $substr) !== false;
            }
	    $ext = isset($_GET["end"]) ? $_GET["end"] : '.php';
            if(isset($_GET['view'])) {
                if(containsStr($_GET['view'], 'tek') || containsStr($_GET['view'], 'pedago')) {
                    echo 'Here you go!';
                    include $_GET['view'] . $ext;
